Whitney anukramaс╣З─л

[ek─Бda┼Ыa v─Бi triguс╣З─Бni. a of 1-27. 1-p. yajur br─Бhmy anuс╣гс╣нubh; b of 7-27. 3-p. nicс╣Ыd g─Бyatr─л; 1 c. praj─Бpaty─Б g─Бyatr─л; d of 1-27. 3-p. pr─Бj─Бpaty─Б triс╣гс╣нubh; c of 2-4, 9, l7, 19, 24. ─Бsur─л jagat─л; c of 5, 7, 8, 10, 11, 13, 18. ─Бsur─л triс╣гс╣нubh; c of 6, 12, 14-16, 20-23, 27. ─Бsur─л pan╠Дkti; c of 25, 26. ─Бsur─л bс╣Ыhat─л.]

Whitney

Comment

тМКThe discrepancy in the numeration of the subdivisions of the pary─Бya, as between the Bombay edition (which follows the Old Anukr.) and the Berlin edition, is of the same kind as in pary─Бya 5, above, and the explanation given above (p. 794, top) may be consulted. The numbers of the avas─Бnas as given by SPP. are added by me in ell-brackets.тМЛ

An imprecation on an enemy

режрез рдЬрд┐рддрдорд╕реНрдорд╛рдХрдореБрджреНрднрд┐рдиреНрдирдорд╕реНрдорд╛рдХрдореГрддрдорд╕реНрдорд╛рдХрдВ рддреЗрдЬреЛрд╜рд╕реНрдорд╛рдХрдореН ...{Loading}...
Whitney
Translation
  1. тМК1.тМЛ Ours [is] what is conquered, ours what has shot up, ours right
    (с╣Ыt├б), ours brilliancy, ours br├бhman, ours heaven (sv├аr), ours the
    sacrifice, ours cattle, ours progeny, ours heroes. тМК2.тМЛ From that we
    disportion him yonder: so-and-so, of such-and-such lineage, son of
    such-and-such mother, who is yonder; тМК3.тМЛ let him not be released from
    the fetter of seizure. тМК4.тМЛ Of him now (id├бm) I involve the splendor,
    brilliancy, breath, lifetime; now I make him fall downward.
Notes

Here is again a partial correspondence with x. 5. 36. Compare also
─Аpast. iv. 15. 3. The addition yajus to the name br─Бhmy anuс╣гс╣нubh (48
syllables) in the Anukr. seems, тМКin the light of the corresponding
expression at xvii. 1. 22, 23, intended to inform us that subdivision
a is a yajus; but it is not apparent why the author should give
this bit of information, which is (of its kind) so isolated: cf. third
note to xv. 5. 7тМЛ.

Griffith

Whatever we have gained, whatever hath accrued to us, our Right, our energy, our Devotion, our heavenly light, our sacrifice, our domestic animals, our offspring, our men,–from all share herein we exclude Such-an-one, descendant of Such- an-one, son of Such-a-woman. Let him not be freed from the noose of Grahi. Here I bind up his splendour, his energy, his vital breath, his life, and cast him down beneath me.
